## User

In this part, you will implement the PageRank algorithm (§2.1) (or the Wikipedia version), which is an algorithm used by search engines like Google to evaluate the quality of links to a webpage. The algorithm can be summarized as follows:

Set initial rank of each page to be 1.
On each iteration, each page p contributes to its outgoing neighbors a value of rank(p)/(# of outgoing neighbors of p).
Update each page's rank to be 0.15 + 0.85 * (sum of contributions).
Go to next iteration.
In this assignment, we will run the algorithm on the. Berkeley-Stanford web graph dataset. Each line in the dataset consists of a page and one of its neighbors. Ask the AI agent to decompress the downloaded .gz dataset.

If you do it manually, you should use the following commands:

$ wget https://snap.stanford.edu/data/web-BerkStan.txt.gz
$ gunzip web-BerkStan.txt.gz
In this part, always run the algorithm for a total of 10 iterations. However, for debugging purpose, you may use a smaller iteration number, say 3 or 4 so that you don't need to wait for too long to see the result.

Your algorithm should initialize ranks only from pages that have outgoing links and only keep pages that receive contributions in each iteration.

This part features four tasks as follows:

Task 1. Write a PySpark application that implements the PageRank algorithm. Your code should use both the two CPU cores on your VM. Your PageRank application should output the following two results:
Print the first 50 rows with the highest ranks;
Save the computed results as a csv file;
Save the measured time result as a separate log file. 

---

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 17.2s)

_Thinking:_

The user wants me to write a PySpark PageRank application. Let me create the implementation based on the requirements:

1. Set initial rank of each page to 1
2. Each page p contributes rank(p)/(# outgoing neighbors) to each neighbor
3. New rank = 0.15 + 0.85 * (sum of contributions)
4. Run for 10 iterations
5. Initialize ranks only from pages with outgoing links
6. Only keep pages that receive contributions
7. Use both CPU cores
8. Output: top 50 rows by rank, save as CSV, save timing log

Let me write the PySpark application.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark import SparkContext\nimport time\nimport csv\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    sc = SparkContext(\"local[2]\", \"PageRank\")\n    \n    raw_lines = sc.textFile(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_lines.filter(lambda line: not line.startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda line: line.strip().split(\"\\t\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda parts: (int(parts[0]), int(parts[1]))) \\\n                     .distinct()\n    \n    out_links = edges.groupByKey()\n    \n    num_pages = out_links.count()\n    \n    ranks = out_links.mapValues(lambda neighbors: 1.0)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contributions = ranks.flatMap(\n            lambda page_rank: [\n                (neighbor, page_rank[1] / len(page_rank[0]))\n                for neighbor in page_rank[0]\n            ]\n        )\n        \n        ranks = contributions.reduceByKey(lambda a, b: a + b) \\\n                             .mapValues(lambda contrib: 0.15 + DAMPING * contrib)\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.takeOrdered(50, key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n        print(f\"{rank_value:<15.6f} {page_id:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        writer = csv.writer(f)\n        writer.writerow([\"page_id\", \"rank\"])\n        for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n            writer.writerow([page_id, rank_value])\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    sc.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.
```

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 3.0s)

Now let me run the application:



**Tool: todowrite**

**Input:**
```json

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 19.7s)

_Thinking:_

The error is in the flatMap lambda - after the first iteration, `ranks` becomes `(page_id, rank_value)` tuples (not `(page_id, (neighbors, rank))` tuples). I need to join the ranks back with the out_links on each iteration. Let me fix the PageRank implementation.

The standard PageRank approach in Spark is:
1. Start with `out_links` = RDD of (page_id, [neighbors])
2. Initialize `ranks` = RDD of (page_id, 1.0)
3. Each iteration:
   - Join ranks with out_links to get (page_id, (rank, neighbors))
   - flatMap to create contributions: (neighbor, rank / num_neighbors)
   - reduceByKey to sum contributions
   - mapValues to apply damping formula

Let me rewrite the code properly.


The issue is that after the first iteration, `ranks` loses the neighbor information. I need to join ranks with out_links each iteration. Let me fix the code:



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark import SparkContext\nimport time\nimport csv\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    sc = SparkContext(\"local[2]\", \"PageRank\")\n    \n    raw_lines = sc.textFile(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_lines.filter(lambda line: not line.startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda line: line.strip().split(\"\\t\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda parts: (int(parts[0]), int(parts[1]))) \\\n                     .distinct()\n    \n    out_links = edges.groupByKey().cache()\n    \n    num_pages = out_links.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = out_links.mapValues(lambda neighbors: 1.0)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = out_links.join(ranks).flatMap(\n            lambda page_links_rank: [\n                (neighbor, page_links_rank[1][1] / len(page_links_rank[1][0]))\n                for neighbor in page_links_rank[1][0]\n            ]\n        )\n        \n        ranks = contribs.reduceByKey(lambda a, b: a + b) \\\n                        .mapValues(lambda contrib: 0.15 + DAMPING * contrib)\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.takeOrdered(50, key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n        print(f\"{rank_value:<15.6f} {page_id:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        writer = csv.writer(f)\n        writer.writerow([\"page_id\", \"rank\"])\n        for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n            writer.writerow([page_id, rank_value])\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    sc.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}
```

```
Wrote file successfully.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark import SparkContext\nimport time\nimport csv\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    sc = SparkContext(\"local[2]\", \"PageRank\")\n    \n    raw_lines = sc.textFile(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_lines.filter(lambda line: not line.startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda line: line.strip().split(\"\\t\")) \\\n                     .map(lambda parts: (int(parts[0]), int(parts[1]))) \\\n                     .distinct()\n    \n    out_links = edges.groupByKey().cache()\n    \n    num_pages = out_links.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = out_links.mapValues(lambda neighbors: 1.0)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = out_links.join(ranks).flatMap(\n            lambda page_links_rank: [\n                (neighbor, page_links_rank[1][1] / len(page_links_rank[1][0]))\n                for neighbor in page_links_rank[1][0]\n            ]\n        )\n        \n        ranks = contribs.reduceByKey(lambda a, b: a + b) \\\n                        .mapValues(lambda contrib: 0.15 + DAMPING * contrib)\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.takeOrdered(50, key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n        print(f\"{rank_value:<15.6f} {page_id:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        writer = csv.writer(f)\n        writer.writerow([\"page_id\", \"rank\"])\n        for page_id, rank_value in top_50:\n            writer.writerow([page_id, rank_value])\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    sc.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 28.4s)

_Thinking:_

The workers are crashing, likely due to memory issues. The dataset is large (7.6M edges) and the join operation creates a lot of data. Let me optimize the approach - instead of using join which creates large intermediate data, I should use a more memory-efficient approach.

The issue is that `out_links.join(ranks)` creates a very large RDD with all the neighbor lists duplicated. For 7.6M edges with large neighbor lists, this can cause memory issues.

Let me rewrite to use a more efficient approach - perhaps using DataFrames or a different RDD strategy that avoids the expensive join.

Actually, looking more carefully, the problem might be that the neighbor lists are very large for some pages, and when we join and then flatMap, we're creating millions of tuples. Let me try a different approach:

1. Use broadcast variables for the ranks (but ranks is too large for broadcast)
2. Use a different join strategy
3. Or use DataFrames which might be more optimized

Let me try using DataFrames instead, which should be more memory efficient.

Actually, let me think about this differently. The issue is memory. With 7.6M edges, when we do `out_links.join(ranks)`, we get tuples like `(page_id, (neighbors_list, rank))`. Then flatMap creates one tuple per edge. With 7.6M edges, that's fine.

The real issue might be that `out_links` has pages with very large neighbor lists, and the groupByKey is creating very large values. Let me check if there are pages with extremely high out-degrees.

Actually, let me try a simpler approach: use DataFrames and the more optimized Catalyst optimizer.

The Python workers are crashing due to memory issues with the large dataset. Let me optimize using DataFrames:



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, sum as sql_sum\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    from pyspark.sql.functions import split, trim\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    out_links = edges.groupBy(\"src\").agg(\n        sql_sum(\"dst\").alias(\"dummy\"),\n    )\n    \n    out_degrees = edges.groupBy(\"src\").count().withColumnRenamed(\"count\", \"out_degree\")\n    \n    num_pages = out_degrees.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = out_degrees.select(\"src\").withColumn(\"rank\", lit(1.0))\n    \n    from pyspark.sql.functions import lit\n    \n    ranks = out_degrees.select(\"src\").withColumn(\"rank\", lit(1.0))\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = edges.join(ranks, edges.src == ranks.src) \\\n                        .select(\"dst\", (col(\"rank\") / col(\"out_degree\")).alias(\"contribution\"))\n        \n        ranks = contribs.groupBy(\"dst\").agg(\n            sql_sum(\"contribution\").alias(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).withColumn(\n            \"rank\", lit(0.15) + lit(DAMPING) * col(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"src\"), \"rank\")\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.orderBy(col(\"rank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['rank']:<15.6f} {row['src']:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        f.write(\"page_id,rank\\n\")\n        for row in top_50:\n            f.write(f\"{row['src']},{row['rank']}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}

\\\n        .appName(\"PageRank\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    out_degrees = edges.groupBy(\"src\").count().withColumnRenamed(\"count\", \"out_degree\")\n    \n    num_pages = out_degrees.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks =    ).select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"src\"), \"rank\")\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 20.4s)

The issue is that after the first iteration, the `out_degree` column is lost. I need to persist it and rejoin each iteration:



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, sum as sql_sum, split, trim, lit\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    out_degrees = edges.groupBy(\"src\").count().withColumnRenamed(\"count\", \"out_degree\")\n    \n    num_pages = out_degrees.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = out_degrees.select(\"src\", \"out_degree\").withColumn(\"rank\", lit(1.0))\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = ranks.join(edges, \"src\") \\\n                        .select(\"dst\", (col(\"rank\") / col(\"out_degree\")).alias(\"contribution\"))\n        \n        new_ranks = contribs.groupBy(\"dst\").agg(\n            sql_sum(\"contribution\").alias(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).withColumn(\n            \"rank\", lit(0.15) + lit(DAMPING) * col(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"src\"), \"rank\")\n        \n        ranks = new_ranks.join(out_degrees, \"src\", \"inner\")\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.orderBy(col(\"rank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['rank']:<15.6f} {row['src']:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        f.write(\"page_id,rank\\n\")\n        for row in top_50:\n            f.write(f\"{row['src']},{row['rank']}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}
```

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, sum as sql_sum, split, trim, lit\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"2g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    out_degrees = edges.groupBy(\"src\").count().withColumnRenamed(\"count\", \"out_degree\")\n    \n    num_pages = out_degrees.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = out_degrees.select(\"src\", \"out_degree\").withColumn(\"rank\", lit(1.0))\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = ranks.join(edges, \"src\") \\\n                        .select(\"dst\", (col(\"rank\") / col(\"out_degree\")).alias(\"contribution\"))\n        \n        new_ranks = contribs.groupBy(\"dst\").agg(\n            sql_sum(\"contribution\").alias(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).withColumn(\n            \"rank\", lit(0.15) + lit(DAMPING) * col(\"sum_contrib\")\n        ).select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"src\"), \"rank\")\n        \n        ranks = new_ranks.join(out_degrees, \"src\", \"inner\")\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages processed\")\n    \n    end_time = time.time()\n    elapsed = end_time - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.orderBy(col(\"rank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['rank']:<15.6f} {row['src']:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        f.write(\"page_id,rank\\n\")\n        for row in top_50:\n            f.write(f\"{row['src']},{row['rank']}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 53.7s)

_Thinking:_

The process seems to have been killed or crashed. The DataFrame approach with joins is likely too memory-intensive. Let me rewrite using RDDs which are more memory-efficient for this type of iterative algorithm. The key issue is that with 7.6M edges and limited memory, the join operations are causing OOM.

I should use a more efficient RDD-based approach that:
1. Avoids joins - instead uses flatMap to distribute contributions
2. Caches only what's necessary
3. Uses broadcast variables if needed
4. Minimizes memory usage

Let me write a cleaner RDD-based version.


The process crashed likely due to memory constraints. Let me rewrite with a more memory-efficient RDD approach:



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark import SparkContext\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    sc = SparkContext(\"local[2]\", \"PageRank\")\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"WARN\")\n    \n    lines = sc.textFile(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    links = lines.filter(lambda l: not l.startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                 .map(lambda l: l.strip().split(\"\\t\")) \\\n                 .filter(lambda p: len(p) == 2 and p[0] != \"\" and p[1] != \"\") \\\n                 .map(lambda p: (int(p[0]), int(p[1]))) \\\n                 .distinct() \\\n                 .groupByKey() \\\n                 .cache()\n    \n    num_pages = links.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = links.mapValues(lambda _: 1.0)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = links.join(ranks).flatMap(\n            lambda x: [(dest, x[1][1] / len(x[1][0])) for dest in x[1][0]]\n        )\n        \n        ranks = contribs.reduceByKey(lambda a, b: a + b) \\\n                        .mapValues(lambda s: 0.15 + DAMPING * s)\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {time.time() - start_time:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.takeOrdered(50, key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for page_id, rank_val in top_50:\n        print(f\"{rank_val:<15.6f} {page_id:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        f.write(\"page_id,rank\\n\")\n        for page_id, rank_val in top_50:\n            f.write(f\"{page_id},{rank_val}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    sc.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"

```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark import SparkConf, SparkContext\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    conf = SparkConf() \\\n        .setAppName(\"PageRank\") \\\n        .setMaster(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .set(\"spark.local.dir\", \"/home/ubuntu/spark-tmp\") \\\n        .set(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .set(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .set(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\")\n    \n    sc = SparkContext(conf=conf)\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"WARN\")\n    \n    lines = sc.textFile(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    links = lines.filter(lambda l: not l.startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                 .map(lambda l: l.strip().split(\"\\t\")) \\\n                 .filter(lambda p: len(p) == 2 and p[0] != \"\" and p[1] != \"\") \\\n                 .map(lambda p: (int(p[0]), int(p[1]))) \\\n                 .distinct() \\\n                 .groupByKey() \\\n                 .cache()\n    \n    num_pages = links.count()\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    ranks = links.mapValues(lambda _: 1.0)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        contribs = links.join(ranks).flatMap(\n            lambda x: [(dest, x[1][1] / len(x[1][0])) for dest in x[1][0]]\n        )\n        \n        ranks = contribs.reduceByKey(lambda a, b: a + b) \\\n                        .mapValues(lambda s: 0.15 + DAMPING * s)\n        \n        ranks.cache()\n        count = ranks.count()\n        ranks.unpersist()\n        \n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {time.time() - start_time:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks.takeOrdered(50, key=lambda x: -x[1])\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for page_id, rank_val in top_50:\n        print(f\"{rank_val:<15.6f} {page_id:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    with open(csv_path, \"w\", newline=\"\") as f:\n        f.write(\"page_id,rank\\n\")\n        for page_id, rank_val in top_50:\n            f.write(f\"{page_id},{rank_val}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    sc.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 22.4s)

_Thinking:_

DuckDB installed. Now I need to write a DuckDB-based PageRank implementation. Let me think about the approach:

1. Load the dataset into DuckDB
2. Create tables for edges and ranks
3. Run iterative PageRank using SQL
4. Measure time
5. Save top 50 to CSV
6. Save timing to log file

The key challenge is implementing iterative PageRank in SQL. I'll need to:
- Load edges into a table
- Initialize ranks
- For each iteration:
  - Calculate contributions from each page to its neighbors
  - Sum contributions per destination page
  - Update ranks with damping factor
- After 10 iterations, get top 50

Let me write the code.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import duckdb\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    con = duckdb.connect()\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges (src BIGINT, dst BIGINT)\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        COPY edges FROM 'web-BerkStan.txt' \n        (DELIMITER '\\t', HEADER false, SKIP 4, \n         COLUMNS (src BIGINT, dst BIGINT))\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges_distinct AS \n        SELECT DISTINCT src, dst FROM edges\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"DROP TABLE edges\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE out_degrees AS \n        SELECT src, COUNT(*) as out_degree \n        FROM edges_distinct \n        GROUP BY src\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    num_pages = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM out_degrees\").fetchone()[0]\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE ranks AS \n        SELECT src, 1.0 as rank \n        FROM out_degrees\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE contributions AS\n            SELECT e.dst, r.rank / o.out_degree as contribution\n            FROM edges_distinct e\n            JOIN ranks r ON e.src = r.src\n            JOIN out_degrees o ON e.src = o.src\n        \"\"\")\n        \n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE new_ranks AS\n            SELECT dst as src, 0.15 + ? * SUM(contribution) as rank\n            FROM contributions\n            GROUP BY dst\n        \"\"\", [DAMPING])\n        \n        con.execute(\"DROP TABLE ranks\")\n        con.execute(\"CREATE TABLE ranks AS SELECT * FROM new_ranks\")\n        \n        count = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ranks\").fetchone()[0]\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {elapsed:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = con.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT src, rank FROM ranks \n        ORDER BY rank DESC \n        LIMIT 50\n    \"\"\").fetchall()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row[1]:<15.6f} {row[0]:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_duckdb_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    con.execute(f\"\"\"\n        COPY (\n            SELECT src as page_id, rank FROM ranks \n            ORDER BY rank DESC \n            LIMIT 50\n        ) TO '{csv_path}' (HEADER, DELIMITER ',')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    con.close()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_duckdb.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.
```

* SUM(contribution) as rank\n            FROM contributions\n            GROUP BY dst\n        \"\"\", [DAMPING])\n        \n        con.execute(\"DROP TABLE ranks\")\n        con.execute(\"CREATE TABLE ranks AS SELECT * FROM new_ranks\")\n        \n        count = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ranks\").fetchone()[0]\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {elapsed:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = con.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT src, rank FROM ranks \n        ORDER BY rank DESC \n        LIMIT 50\n    \"\"\").fetchall()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row[1]:<15.6f} {row[0]:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_duckdb_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    con.execute(f\"\"\"\n        COPY (\n            SELECT src as page_id, rank FROM ranks \n            ORDER BY rank DESC \n            LIMIT 50\n        ) TO '{csv_path}' (HEADER, DELIMITER ',')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    con.close()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_duckdb.py"
}

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 4.9s)

_Thinking:_

The error is about the COLUMNS syntax. In DuckDB, the COLUMNS clause doesn't use type annotations. Let me fix the COPY statement.

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_duckdb.py",
  "newString": "    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        COPY edges FROM 'web-BerkStan.txt' \n        (DELIMITER '\\t', HEADER false, SKIP 4, \n         COLUMNS (src, dst))\n    \"\"\")",
  "oldString": "    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        COPY edges FROM 'web-BerkStan.txt' \n        (DELIMITER '\\t', HEADER false, SKIP 4, \n         COLUMNS (src BIGINT, dst BIGINT))\n    \"\"\")"
}
```

Edit applied successfully.

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 20.1s)

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import duckdb\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    con = duckdb.connect()\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE raw_lines (line VARCHAR)\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        COPY raw_lines FROM 'web-BerkStan.txt' (DELIMITER '\\n')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges AS\n        SELECT \n            CAST(str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[1] AS BIGINT) as src,\n            CAST(str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[2] AS BIGINT) as dst\n        FROM raw_lines\n        WHERE line NOT LIKE '#%'\n          AND str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[1] != ''\n          AND str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[2] != ''\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"DROP TABLE raw_lines\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges_distinct AS \n        SELECT DISTINCT src, dst FROM edges\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"DROP TABLE edges\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE out_degrees AS \n        SELECT src, COUNT(*) as out_degree \n        FROM edges_distinct \n        GROUP BY src\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    num_pages = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM out_degrees\").fetchone()[0]\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE ranks AS \n        SELECT src, 1.0 as rank \n        FROM out_degrees\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE contributions AS\n            SELECT e.dst, r.rank / o.out_degree as contribution\n            FROM edges_distinct e\n            JOIN ranks r ON e.src = r.src\n            JOIN out_degrees o ON e.src = o.src\n        \"\"\")\n        \n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE new_ranks AS\n            SELECT dst as src, 0.15 + ? * SUM(contribution) as rank\n            FROM contributions\n            GROUP BY dst\n        \"\"\", [DAMPING])\n        \n        con.execute(\"DROP TABLE ranks\")\n        con.execute(\"CREATE TABLE ranks AS SELECT * FROM new_ranks\")\n        \n        count = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ranks\").fetchone()[0]\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {elapsed:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = con.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT src, rank FROM ranks \n        ORDER BY rank DESC \n        LIMIT 50\n    \"\"\").fetchall()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row[1]:<15.6f} {row[0]:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_duckdb_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    con.execute(f\"\"\"\n        COPY (\n            SELECT src as page_id, rank FROM ranks \n            ORDER BY rank DESC \n            LIMIT 50\n        ) TO '{csv_path}' (HEADER, DELIMITER ',')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    con.close()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_duckdb.py"
}

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import duckdb\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    con = duckdb.connect()\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE raw_lines (line VARCHAR)\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        COPY raw_lines FROM 'web-BerkStan.txt' (DELIMITER '\\n')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges AS\n        SELECT \n            CAST(str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[1] AS BIGINT) as src,\n            CAST(str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[2] AS BIGINT) as dst\n        FROM raw_lines\n        WHERE line NOT LIKE '#%'\n          AND str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[1] != ''\n          AND str_split_trim(line, '\\t')[2] != ''\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"DROP TABLE raw_lines\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE edges_distinct AS \n        SELECT DISTINCT src, dst FROM edges\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"DROP TABLE edges\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE out_degrees AS \n        SELECT src, COUNT(*) as out_degree \n        FROM edges_distinct \n        GROUP BY src\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    num_pages = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM out_degrees\").fetchone()[0]\n    print(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\")\n    \n    con.execute(\"\"\"\n        CREATE TABLE ranks AS \n        SELECT src, 1.0 as rank \n        FROM out_degrees\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    DAMPING = 0.85\n    \n    for iteration in range(NUM_ITERATIONS):\n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE contributions AS\n            SELECT e.dst, r.rank / o.out_degree as contribution\n            FROM edges_distinct e\n            JOIN ranks r ON e.src = r.src\n            JOIN out_degrees o ON e.src = o.src\n        \"\"\")\n        \n        con.execute(\"\"\"\n            CREATE OR REPLACE TEMP TABLE new_ranks AS\n            SELECT dst as src, 0.15 + ? * SUM(contribution) as rank\n            FROM contributions\n            GROUP BY dst\n        \"\"\", [DAMPING])\n        \n        con.execute(\"DROP TABLE ranks\")\n        con.execute(\"CREATE TABLE ranks AS SELECT * FROM new_ranks\")\n        \n        count = con.execute(\"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ranks\").fetchone()[0]\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"Iteration {iteration + 1}: {count} pages, time so far: {elapsed:.1f}s\")\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nTotal computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    top_50 = con.execute(\"\"\"\n        SELECT src, rank FROM ranks \n        ORDER BY rank DESC \n        LIMIT 50\n    \"\"\").fetchall()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row[1]:<15.6f} {row[0]:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_duckdb_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    con.execute(f\"\"\"\n        COPY (\n            SELECT src as page_id, rank FROM ranks \n            ORDER BY rank DESC \n            LIMIT 50\n        ) TO '{csv_path}' (HEADER, DELIMITER ',')\n    \"\"\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Total pages with outgoing links: {num_pages}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Pages in final iteration: {count}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Damping factor: {DAMPING}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    con.close()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_duckdb.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 19.4s)

_Thinking:_

The user wants me to complete Task 3, which involves:
1. Writing a Spark program using GraphFrames' built-in PageRank library
2. Measuring the time for 10 iterations
3. Saving top 50 rows as CSV
4. Saving time results as a log file
5. Saving the entire session transcript as a markdown file

Let me write the GraphFrames PageRank implementation first.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, split, trim, lit\nfrom graphframes import GraphFrame\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank-GraphFrames\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.jars.packages\", \"graphframes:graphframes:0.8.3-spark3.5-s_2.12\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    vertices = edges.select(col(\"src\").alias(\"id\")).union(\n        edges.select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"id\"))\n    ).distinct()\n    \n    num_vertices = vertices.count()\n    num_edges = edges.count()\n    print(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}, Edges: {num_edges}\")\n    \n    g = GraphFrame(vertices, edges)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    RESET_PROBABILITY = 0.15\n    \n    result = g.pageRank(resetProbability=RESET_PROBABILITY, maxIter=NUM_ITERATIONS)\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    ranks_df = result.vertices.select(\"id\", \"pagerank\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['pagerank']:<15.6f} {row['id']:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_graphframes_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50) \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"id\", \"page_id\") \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"pagerank\", \"rank\") \\\n        .write \\\n        .option(\"header\", \"true\") \\\n        .csv(csv_path, mode=\"overwrite\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Edges: {num_edges}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Reset probability: {RESET_PROBABILITY}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_graphframes.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, split, trim, lit\nfrom graphframes import GraphFrame\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank-GraphFrames\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.jars.packages\", \"graphframes:graphframes:0.8.3-spark3.5-s_2.12\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n    \n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n    \n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n    \n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n    \n    vertices = edges.select(col(\"src\").alias(\"id\")).union(\n        edges.select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"id\"))\n    ).distinct()\n    \n    num_vertices = vertices.count()\n    num_edges = edges.count()\n    print(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}, Edges: {num_edges}\")\n    \n    g = GraphFrame(vertices, edges)\n    \n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    RESET_PROBABILITY = 0.15\n    \n    result = g.pageRank(resetProbability=RESET_PROBABILITY, maxIter=NUM_ITERATIONS)\n    \n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n    \n    ranks_df = result.vertices.select(\"id\", \"pagerank\")\n    \n    top_50 = ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n    \n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['pagerank']:<15.6f} {row['id']:<15}\")\n    \n    output_dir = \"pagerank_graphframes_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    \n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50) \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"id\", \"page_id\") \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"pagerank\", \"rank\") \\\n        .write \\\n        .option(\"header\", \"true\") \\\n        .csv(csv_path, mode=\"overwrite\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n    \n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Edges: {num_edges}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Reset probability: {RESET_PROBABILITY}\\n\")\n    \n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n    \n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_graphframes.py"
}
```

Wrote file successfully.

# GraphFrames: graph algorithms at scale

This is a package for graphs processing and analytics on scale. It is built on top of Apache Spark and relies on DataFrame abstraction. It provides built-in and easy to use distributed graph algorithms as well as a flexible APIs like `Pregel` or `AggregateMessages` to make custom graph processing. Users can write highly expressive queries by leveraging the DataFrame API, combined with a new API for network motif finding. The user also benefits from DataFrame performance optimizations within the Spark SQL engine. GraphFrames works in Java, Scala, and Python.

## GraphFrames usecases

There are some popular use cases when GraphFrames is almost irreplaceable, including, but not limited to:

- Compliance analytics with a scalable shortest paths algorithm and motif analysis;
- Anti-fraud with scalable cycles detection in large networks;
- Identity resolution on the scale of billions with highly efficient connected components;
- Search result ranking with a distributed, Pregel-based PageRank;
- Clustering huge graphs with Label Propagation and Power Iteration Clustering;
- Building a knowledge graph systems with Property Graph Model.

## Documentation

- [Installation](https://graphframes.io/02-quick-start/01-installation.html)
- [Creating Graphs](https://graphframes.io/04-user-guide/01-creating-graphframes.html)
- [Basic Graph Manipulations](https://graphframes.io/04-user-guide/02-basic-operations.html)
- [Centrality Metrics](http

```

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 18.3s)

The new coordinates are `io.graphframes:graphframes-spark3_2.13:0.11.0`. Let me update the code:



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, split, trim\nfrom graphframes import GraphFrame\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank-GraphFrames\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.jars.packages\", \"io.graphframes:graphframes-spark3_2.13:0.11.0\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n\n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n\n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n\n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n\n    vertices = edges.select(col(\"src\").alias(\"id\")).union(\n        edges.select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"id\"))\n    ).distinct()\n\n    num_vertices = vertices.count()\n    num_edges = edges.count()\n    print(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}, Edges: {num_edges}\")\n\n    g = GraphFrame(vertices, edges)\n\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    RESET_PROBABILITY = 0.15\n\n    result = g.pageRank(resetProbability=RESET_PROBABILITY, maxIter=NUM_ITERATIONS)\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n\n    ranks_df = result.vertices.select(\"id\", \"pagerank\")\n\n    top_50 = ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n\n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['pagerank']:<15.6f} {row['id']:<15}\")\n\n    output_dir = \"pagerank_graphframes_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50) \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"id\", \"page_id\") \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"pagerank\", \"rank\") \\\n        .write \\\n        .option(\"header\", \"true\") \\\n        .csv(csv_path, mode=\"overwrite\")\n\n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n\n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Edges: {num_edges}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Reset probability: {RESET_PROBABILITY}\\n\")\n\n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n\n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_graphframes.py"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.
```

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "from pyspark.sql import SparkSession\nfrom pyspark.sql.functions import col, split, trim\nfrom graphframes import GraphFrame\nimport time\nimport os\n\ndef main():\n    spark = SparkSession.builder \\\n        .appName(\"PageRank-GraphFrames\") \\\n        .master(\"local[2]\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.jars\", \"/tmp/graphframes-spark3_2.13-0.11.0.jar,/tmp/graphframes-graphx-spark3_2.13-0.11.0.jar\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.sql.shuffle.partitions\", \"4\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.driver.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .config(\"spark.executor.memory\", \"3g\") \\\n        .getOrCreate()\n\n    sc = spark.sparkContext\n    sc.setLogLevel(\"ERROR\")\n\n    raw_df = spark.read.text(\"web-BerkStan.txt\")\n\n    edges = raw_df.filter(~col(\"value\").startswith(\"#\")) \\\n                  .select(split(trim(col(\"value\")), \"\\t\").alias(\"parts\")) \\\n                  .filter(col(\"parts\").isNotNull() & (col(\"parts\").getItem(0) != \"\")) \\\n                  .select(\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(0).cast(\"long\").alias(\"src\"),\n                      col(\"parts\").getItem(1).cast(\"long\").alias(\"dst\")\n                  ) \\\n                  .dropDuplicates()\n\n    vertices = edges.select(col(\"src\").alias(\"id\")).union(\n        edges.select(col(\"dst\").alias(\"id\"))\n    ).distinct()\n\n    num_vertices = vertices.count()\n    num_edges = edges.count()\n    print(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}, Edges: {num_edges}\")\n\n    g = GraphFrame(vertices, edges)\n\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    NUM_ITERATIONS = 10\n    RESET_PROBABILITY = 0.15\n\n    result = g.pageRank(resetProbability=RESET_PROBABILITY, maxIter=NUM_ITERATIONS)\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"Total computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\")\n\n    ranks_df = result.vertices.select(\"id\", \"pagerank\")\n\n    top_50 = ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50).collect()\n\n    print(\"\\nTop 50 pages by PageRank:\")\n    print(f\"{'Rank':<15} {'Page ID':<15}\")\n    print(\"-\" * 30)\n    for row in top_50:\n        print(f\"{row['pagerank']:<15.6f} {row['id']:<15}\")\n\n    output_dir = \"pagerank_graphframes_output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    csv_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_results.csv\")\n    ranks_df.orderBy(col(\"pagerank\").desc()).limit(50) \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"id\", \"page_id\") \\\n        .withColumnRenamed(\"pagerank\", \"rank\") \\\n        .write \\\n        .option(\"header\", \"true\") \\\n        .csv(csv_path, mode=\"overwrite\")\n\n    print(f\"\\nResults saved to {csv_path}\")\n\n    log_path = os.path.join(output_dir, \"pagerank_time.log\")\n    with open(log_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(f\"PageRank computation time: {elapsed:.2f} seconds\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Dataset: web-BerkStan.txt\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Vertices: {num_vertices}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Edges: {num_edges}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Iterations: {NUM_ITERATIONS}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Reset probability: {RESET_PROBABILITY}\\n\")\n\n    print(f\"Timing log saved to {log_path}\")\n\n    spark.stop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "/home/ubuntu/pagerank_graphframes.py"
}

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6 Plus · 34.8s)

_Thinking:_

The GraphFrames PageRank completed successfully. Now I need to note that the results are slightly different from Task 1 and Task 2. This is because GraphFrames uses a slightly different PageRank implementation - it initializes all vertices (including those without outgoing links) with the same rank, and the random teleport probability distributes differently.

Let me compare the results:

Task 1 (PySpark custom) and Task 2 (DuckDB) - identical results:
1. 272919 - 6531.324624
2. 438238 - 4335.323159
3. 571448 - 2383.897607

Task 3 (GraphFrames):
1. 272919 - 6649.555171
2. 438238 - 5198.922569
3. 210376 - 3550.046177

The differences are because:
1. GraphFrames includes ALL vertices (685,230) including sink nodes (pages with no outgoing links)
2. The custom implementation only keeps pages that receive contributions
3. GraphFrames handles dangling nodes differently

The top page (272919) is consistent across all three, which validates the general correctness. The rank values differ because of the different handling of dangling nodes and the full vertex set.

Now I need to create the session transcript markdown file covering all three tasks.

Page 272919 - Rank: 6531.324624\n  2. Page 438238 - Rank: 4335.323159\n  3. Page 571448 - Rank: 2383.897607\n\n### Output Files\n- `pagerank_duckdb_output/pagerank_results.csv` - Top 50 pages\n- `pagerank_duckdb_output/pagerank_time.log` - Timing log\n\n---\n\n## Task 3: Spark GraphFrames PageRank\n\n### Setup\n- Downloaded GraphFrames JARs from Maven Central:\n  - `graphframes-spark4_2.13-0.11.0.jar`\n  - `graphframes-graphx-spark4_2.13-0.11.0.jar`\n- GraphFrames 0.11.0 is compatible with Spark 4.x (Scala 2.13)\n\n### Implementation (`pagerank_graphframes.py`)\nUsed GraphFrames built-in PageRank:\n- `g.pageRank(resetProbability=0.15, maxIter=10)`\n- Includes all 685,230 vertices (including sink nodes)\n- Same damping factor (0.15 reset probability = 0.85 damping)\n\n### Results\n- **Computation time: 244.45 seconds**\n- 685,230 vertices, 7,600,595 edges\n- Top 3 pages:\n  1. Page 272919 - Rank: 6649.555171\n  2. Page 438238 - Rank: 5198.922569\n  3. Page 210376 - Rank: 3550.046177\n\n### Note on Result Differences\nGraphFrames results differ slightly from Tasks 1-2 because:\n1. GraphFrames includes **all vertices** (685,230) including sink nodes with no outgoing links\n2. Custom implementations only track pages with outgoing links (680,486)\n3. GraphFrames handles dangling nodes via the built-in random teleport distribution\n4. The #1 ranked page (272919) is consistent across all three implementations\n\n### Output Files\n- `pagerank_graphframes_output/pagerank_results.csv` - Top 50 pages\n- `pagerank_graphframes_output/pagerank_time.log` - Timing log\n\n---\n\n## Performance Comparison\n\n| Implementation | Time | Relative Speed |\n|---|---|---|\n| DuckDB | 7.58s | 1x (fastest) |\n| GraphFrames | 244.45s | 32x slower |\n| PySpark (custom) | 471.19s | 62x slower |\n\n## Key Challenges Encountered\n1. **Disk quota exceeded** when building pyspark from source (Python 3.14 has no pre-built wheels)\n2. **Java version mismatch** - PySpark 4.x requires Java 11+ (system had Java 8)\n3. **Python worker crashes** with RDD `groupByKey` on large dataset due to memory\n4. **GraphFrames JAR download failures** - spark-packages.org was down, had to download manually from Maven Central\n5. **GraphFrames version compatibility** - needed Spark 4 specific JARs (`graphframes-spark4_2.13`)\n",
